# Test Report

Time: 2024-03-29 22:44:44.398769

### Base Program

```py
def reachNumber(target: int) -> int:
    target = abs(target)
    step = 0
    sum = 0
    while sum < target:
        step += 1
        sum += step
    while (sum - target) % 2 != 0:
        step += 1
        sum += step
    return step
```

```json
[40]
```

## Test Case 1

### Modified Program

```py
def reachNumber(target: int) -> int:
    target = abs(target)
    step = 0
    sum = 0
    while sum < target:
        step += 1
        sum += step
    while (sum - target) % 2 != 0:
        step += 1
        sum += step
    return step
```

## Test Case 2

### Modified Program

```py
def reachNumber(var_0: int) -> int:
    var_0 = abs(var_0)
    step = 0
    sum = 0
    while sum < var_0:
        step += 1
        sum += step
    while (sum - var_0) % 2 != 0:
        step += 1
        sum += step
    return step
```

## Test Case 3

### Modified Program

```py
def reachNumber(target: int) -> int:
    target = abs(target)
    step = 0
    sum = 0
    while sum < target:
        step += 1
        sum += step
    while (sum + -target) % 2 != 0:
        step += 1
        sum += step
    return step
```

## Test Case 4

### Modified Program

```py
def reachNumber(var_1: int) -> int:
    var_1 = abs(var_1)
    step = 0
    sum = 0
    while sum < var_1:
        step += 1
        sum += step
    while (sum + -var_1) % 2 != 0:
        step += 1
        sum += step
    return step
```
